(src)="292293"> Banknotes
(trg)="1"> Biyete
(src)="292294"> The Netherlands Antillean guilder ( Dutch : gulden ) is the currency of Curaçao and Sint Maarten , which until 2010 formed the Netherlands Antilles along with Bonaire , Saba , and Sint Eustatius .
(src)="292295"> It is subdivided into 100 cents ( Dutch plural form : centen ) .
(src)="292296"> The guilder was replaced by the US dollar on 1 January 2011 on Bonaire , Saba and Sint Eustatius.[1 ] On Curaçao and Sint Maarten , the Netherlands Antillean guilder is planned to be replaced by the newly created[1 ] Caribbean guilder.[2 ]
(trg)="2"> E Florin Antiano ( hulandes : heldu ) ta e moneda di Kòrsou  i Sint Maarten , ku te ku 2010 a forma e pais  Antias Hulandes , huntu ku Boneiru , Saba  i Sint Eustatius .
(trg)="3"> E ta supdividí den 100 ' cent '  ( hulandes forma plural : centen ) .
(trg)="4"> Desde 1 di januari 2011 e  florin a keda remplasa pa e Dollar Merikano  na Boneiru , Saba i Sint Eustatius . [ 1 ] Na Kòrsou i Sint Maarten , e florin antiyano a keda propone pa wòrdu sustituí pa e resien krea [ 1 ]  Florin Karibense . [ 2 ]
(src)="292297"> In 1986 , Aruba gained a status aparte and thereby left the Netherlands Antilles .
(src)="292298"> Shortly after that , Aruba began to issue its own currency , the Aruban florin , which replaced the Netherlands Antillean guilder at par .
(trg)="5"> Na 1986 , Aruba a haña su status aparte  i a bandona Antias .
(trg)="6"> Poko despues di esaki , Aruba a kuminsa saka su propio moneda , florin Arubiano , kual a remplasa e florin Antiyano kual tabata reina na e tempu ei .
(src)="292299"> In 1892 , the Curaçaosche Bank introduced notes in denominations of 25 and 50 cents , 1 and 2  1⁄2 guilders .
(src)="292300"> This was the only issue of the cent denominations .
(src)="292301"> Notes for 5 , 10 , 25 , 50 , 100 , 250 and 500 guilders followed in 1900 .
(src)="292302"> The 1 and 2  1⁄2 guilder notes were suspended after 1920 but reintroduced by the government in 1942 as muntbiljet .
(trg)="7"> Na 1892 , Banko Kurasoleño a introdusi  biyete nan den denominashon di 25 i 50 cent , 1 i 2 1 ⁄ 2 florin .
(trg)="8"> Esaki tabata e úniko temporada ku a saka cent na biyete .
(trg)="9"> Biyete nan di 5 , 10 , 25 , 50 , 100 , 250 i 500 florin a sigui na 1900 .
(trg)="10"> Biyete nan di 1 i 2 1 ⁄ 2 florin a keda suspende despues di 1920 , pero a wòrdu re-introdusi pa gobiernu na 1942 bou di e nòmber di  muntbiljet .
(src)="292303"> From 1954 , the name " Nederlandse Antillen " appeared on the reverse of the notes of the Curaçaosche Bank and , from 1955 , the muntbiljet (  2  1⁄2 guilders only ) was issued in the name of the Nederlandse Antillen .
(src)="292304"> In 1962 , the bank 's name was changed to the Bank van de Nederlandse Antillen .
(src)="292305"> Starting in 1969 , notes dated 28 AUGUSTUS 1967 began to be introduced .
(src)="292306"> The front of these notes all feature the Statuut monument at front left instead of the allegorical seated woman found on the preceding issues , and on the back there is a new coat of arms.[4 ] In 1970 , a final issue of muntbiljet was made in denominations of both 1 and 2  1⁄2 guilders .
(src)="292307"> The 500 guilder note was not issued after 1962 .
(trg)="11"> Desde 1954 , e nòmber di " Nederlandse Antillen " a kuminsa aparesé riba parti patras di e biyete di Banko Kurasoleño , i , for di 1955 , e muntbiljet ( spesifikamente esun di 2 1 ⁄ 2  florin ) tabata wòrdu saká bou di e nòmber di Nederlandse Antillen .
(trg)="12"> Na 1962 , e banko su nòmber a keda kambia pa kambia na e Banko di Antias Hulandes .
(trg)="13"> Na 1969 , biyete nan ku fecha di 28 di OUGUSTUS 1967 , a keda introdusi .
(trg)="14"> E parti dilanti di e biyete nan aki ta ilustra e monumento di Statut na parti lenks na lugá di e di e muher sintá topa den e biyete nan anterior i riba e parti patras por mira ilustrashon di un eskudo di arma nobo . [ 4 ] Na 1970 , a saka ultimo e muntbiljet den denominashon di 1 i 2 1 ⁄ 2 florin .
(trg)="15"> Produkshon di e biyete di 500 florin a keda deskontinua na 1962 .
(src)="292308"> The 10 guilder bill is illustrated with a kolibrie .
(src)="292309"> Security features include a surface foil tag , an embedded hologram under the hummingbird , and an orange moiré pattern contrasting with the green bill .
(src)="292310"> The 25 guilder bill is illustrated with a flamingo .
(src)="292311"> Security features include a surface foil tag , an embedded hologram under the flamingo , and a green moiré pattern contrasting with the pink bill .
(src)="292312"> The 50 guilder bill has an andes mus on the face .
(src)="292313"> Security features include a surface foil tag , an embedded hologram under the mus , and a green moiré pattern contrasting with the orange bill .
(src)="292314"> The 100 guilder bill has a suikerdiefje on the face .
(src)="292315"> Security features include a surface foil tag , an embedded hologram under the suikerdiefje , and a green moiré pattern contrasting with the brown bill .
(trg)="16"> Biyete di 10 florin ku ilustrashon di un kolibrí .
(trg)="17"> Karakterístika nan di seguridat ta inklui un ' surface foil tag , un ' hologram ' bou di e kolibrí i un ' moiré pattern ' oraño ku por mira den kontrast ku e bèrdè di e biyete .
(trg)="18"> E biyete di 25 florin tin ilustrashon di un flamingo .
(trg)="19"> Karakterístika nan di seguridat ta inklui un ' surface foil tag , un ' hologram ' bou di e flamingo i un ' moiré pattern ' bèrdè ku por mira den kontrast ku e ros di e biyete .
(trg)="20"> E 50 florin di e proyekto di lei tin un cordia di mas di e karu .
(trg)="21"> Karakterístika riba include un base di plachi di etiqueta , un mede programa bou di mas , i un bèrdè more di contact ku e orañe proyekto di lei .
(trg)="22"> E 100 florin pa mil tin un suikerdiefje na karu .
(trg)="23"> Karakterístika riba include un base di plachi di etiqueta , un mede programa bou di e suikerdiefje , i un bèrdè more contact ku e maron proyekto di lei .

(trg)="27"> Coins
(src)="292322"> Notes
(trg)="28"> Notes
(src)="292325"> In Papiamentu , the local language of Aruba , Bonaire and Curaçao , the guilder is called a " florin".[3 ] The ISO-4217 code , ANG , is derived from ANtilliaanse Gulden , while the currency symbol , NAFl , is derived from Netherlands Antilles Florin .
(trg)="29"> Na  Papiamentu , e idioma ofisial di  Aruba , Boneiru  i  Kòrsou , ta yama e florin antiano simplemente ' florin ' [ 3 ] E ISO-4217 code , ANG , ta derivá for di  ANtilliaanse Gulden , mientras ku e signo di e moneda , NAFl , ta derivá for di  Netherlands Antilles Florin .
(src)="292326"> In the 18th century , the Dutch guilder circulated in the Netherlands Antilles .
(src)="292327"> This was supplemented in 1794 by an issue of coins specific for the Dutch holdings in the West Indies .
(src)="292328"> At this time , the guilder was subdivided into 20 stuiver .
(trg)="30"> Den siglo 18 , e Florin Hulandes  tabata sirkula den Antias Hulandes .
(trg)="31"> Esaki a keda suplementa na 1794 pa un moneda krea spesifiko pa e kolonia nan Hulandes den  India Oksidental .
(trg)="32"> Na e momentu ei , e florin tabata wòrdu subdividi den 20 stuiver .
(src)="292329"> Between 1799 and 1828 , the reaal circulated on the islands , with 1 reaal = 6 stuiver or 3  1⁄3 reaal = 1 guilder .
(src)="292330"> The Dutch guilder was reintroduced in 1828 , now subdivided into 100 cents .
(src)="292331"> When currency began once more to be issued specifically for use in the Netherlands Antilles , it was issued in the name of Curaçao , with the first banknotes and coins , denominated in the Dutch currency , introduced in 1892 and 1900 , respectively .
(src)="292332"> The name " Netherlands Antilles " ( Nederlandse Antillen ) was introduced in 1952 .
(trg)="33"> Entre 1799 and 1828 , e  reaal tabata sirkula entre e isla nan , kaminda 1 reaal = 6 stuiver òf 3  1 ⁄ 3 reaal = 1 florin .
(trg)="34"> E florin Hulandes a keda re-introdusí na 1828 , awor subdividi den 100 cent .
(trg)="35"> Na momentu ku moneda nan a kuminsa wòrdu saka mas spesifikamente pa uzo den Antias , e tabata wòrdu saká bou di nòmber di Kòrsou , kaminda ku e prome biyete i munt nan , denomina den moneda Hulandes , a keda introdusi na 1892 i 1900 , respektivamente .
(trg)="36"> E nòmber Antias Hulandes a keda introdusi na 1952 .
(src)="292333"> In 1940 , following the German occupation of the Netherlands , the link to the Dutch currency was broken , with a peg to the U.S. dollar of 1.88585 guilders = 1 dollar established .
(src)="292334"> The peg was adjusted to 1.79 guilders = 1 dollar in 1971 .
(src)="292335"> Since then it has been updated to 1.77 guilders = 1 dollar but unsure of the date .
(trg)="37"> Na 1940 , despues di e okupashon Aleman  di hulanda , e konekshon ku e moneda Hulandes a keda kibrá i a introdusi un konekshon ku e Dollar Merikano  kaminda ku 1.88585 florn = 1 dollar .
(trg)="38"> E konekshon a keda adapta na 1,79 florin = 1 dollar na 1971 .
(trg)="39"> Atraves di tempu esaki a keda adapta na 1.77 florin = 1 dollar .

(src)="292370"> Research Impact Static electricity and magnetism ( c.
(src)="292371"> 1600 ) Electric current ( 18th century ) All electric appliances , dynamos , electric power stations , modern electronics , including electric lighting , television , electric heating , transcranial magnetic stimulation , deep brain stimulation , magnetic tape , loudspeaker , and the compass and lightning rod .
(src)="292372"> Diffraction ( 1665 ) Optics , hence fiber optic cable ( 1840s ) , modern intercontinental communications , and cable TV and internet Germ theory ( 1700 ) Hygiene , leading to decreased transmission of infectious diseases ; antibodies , leading to techniques for disease diagnosis and targeted anticancer therapies .
(src)="292373"> Vaccination ( 1798 ) Leading to the elimination of most infectious diseases from developed countries and the worldwide eradication of smallpox .
(src)="292374"> Photovoltaic effect ( 1839 ) Solar cells ( 1883 ) , hence solar power , solar powered watches , calculators and other devices .
(src)="292375"> The strange orbit of Mercury ( 1859 ) and other research leading to special ( 1905 ) and general relativity ( 1916 ) Satellite-based technology such as GPS ( 1973 ) , satnav and satellite communications[lower-alpha 22 ] Radio waves ( 1887 ) Radio had become used in innumerable ways beyond its better-known areas of telephony , and broadcast television ( 1927 ) and radio ( 1906 ) entertainment .
(src)="292376"> Other uses included  – emergency services , radar ( navigation and weather prediction ) , medicine , astronomy , wireless communications , geophysics , and networking .
(src)="292377"> Radio waves also led researchers to adjacent frequencies such as microwaves , used worldwide for heating and cooking food .
(src)="292378"> Radioactivity ( 1896 ) and antimatter ( 1932 ) Cancer treatment ( 1896 ) , Radiometric dating ( 1905 ) , nuclear reactors ( 1942 ) and weapons ( 1945 ) , mineral exploration , PET scans ( 1961 ) , and medical research ( via isotopic labeling ) X-rays ( 1896 ) Medical imaging , including computed tomography Crystallography and quantum mechanics ( 1900 ) Semiconductor devices ( 1906 ) , hence modern computing and telecommunications including the integration with wireless devices : the mobile phone[lower-alpha 22 ] Plastics ( 1907 ) Starting with Bakelite , many types of artificial polymers for numerous applications in industry and daily life Antibiotics ( 1880s , 1928 ) Salvarsan , Penicillin , doxycycline etc.
(src)="292379"> Nuclear magnetic resonance ( 1930s ) Nuclear magnetic resonance spectroscopy ( 1946 ) , magnetic resonance imaging ( 1971 ) , functional magnetic resonance imaging ( 1990s ) .

(trg)="297"> " After Einstein : Scientific genius is extinct " .
(trg)="298"> Nature .
(trg)="299"> 493 ( 7434 ) : 602 – 602. doi : 10.1038 / 493602a .
(trg)="300"> PMID  23364725 . 
(src)="292712"> Evolution is change in the heritable characteristics of biological populations over successive generations.[1][2 ] Evolutionary processes give rise to biodiversity at every level of biological organisation , including the levels of species , individual organisms , and molecules.[3 ]
(trg)="301"> Evolushon  ta kambio den e  karakterístikanan hereditario di  populashonnan  biológiko  durante di generashonnan  susesivo . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] Prosesonan evolushonario ta kausa  biodiversidat  den tur nivel di  organisashon biológiko , inkluyendo nivelnan di espesienan ,  organismonan  individual , i molekülnan . [ 3 ]
(src)="292713"> All life on Earth shares a common ancestor known as the last universal common ancestor (LUCA),[4][5][6 ] which lived approximately 3.5–3.8 billion years ago,[7 ] although a study in 2015 found " remains of biotic life " from 4.1 billion years ago in ancient rocks in Western Australia.[8][9 ] In July 2016 , scientists reported identifying a set of 355 genes from the LUCA of all organisms living on Earth.[10 ]
(trg)="302"> Tur  bida  riba  Tera  ta komparti un antepasado komun konosí komo e último antepasado komun universal  ( UAKU ) , [ 4 ] [ 5 ] [ 6 ] , ku a biba aproksimadamente 3.5-3.8 bion aña , [ 7 ] aunke un estudio den e aña 2015 a haña " restunan dia  bida biótika " di 4.1 bion aña den piedranan ansiano den Australia Oksidental . [ 8 ] [ 9 ] Na yüli 2016 , sientífikonan a reportá identifikashon di un sèt di 355 genenan  for di e UAKU di tur organismonan  bibu Tera . [ 10 ]
(src)="292714"> Repeated formation of new species ( speciation ) , change within species ( anagenesis ) , and loss of species ( extinction ) throughout the evolutionary history of life on Earth are demonstrated by shared sets of morphological and biochemical traits , including shared DNA sequences.[11 ] These shared traits are more similar among species that share a more recent common ancestor , and can be used to reconstruct a biological " tree of life " based on evolutionary relationships ( phylogenetics ) , using both existing species and fossils .
(src)="292715"> The fossil record includes a progression from early biogenic graphite,[12 ] to microbial mat fossils,[13][14][15 ] to fossilized multicellular organisms .
(src)="292716"> Existing patterns of biodiversity have been shaped both by speciation and by extinction.[16 ] More than 99 percent of all species that ever lived on Earth are estimated to be extinct.[17][18 ] Estimates of Earth 's current species range from 10 to 14 million,[19][20 ] of which about 1.9 million are estimated to have been named[21 ] and 1.6 million documented in a central database to date.[22 ] More recently , in May 2016 , scientists reported that 1 trillion species are estimated to be on Earth currently with only one-thousandth of one percent described.[23 ]
(trg)="303"> Formashon kontinuo di espesianan nobo ( Espesiashon ) , kambio den espesianan ( anagenesis ) , i e pèrdida di espesianan ( ekstinshon ) durante historia evolushonario di bida  riba Tera ta keda demostrá pa sètnan di karakterístikanan  morfológiko  i biokímiko , inkluyendo  sekuensianan di ADN  kompartí . [ 11 ]  E karakteristikanan kompartí aki  ta mas similar entre e sorto ku comparti un otro recent castro komun , i ku e por ta utilisá pa reconecta un biológiko " palu di bida " , bisa den e relacionnan revolution ( ilona ) , aterisando tantu e sorto extende i files .
(trg)="304"> E registro fosil inclui un progreso di tempran biogénicas di grafico , [ 12 ] na microbiana met files , [ 13 ] [ 14 ] [ 15 ] na fosilizados ta organisa multicelulares .
(trg)="305"> Di patras extende di e bioversidat a forma pa e asociacion i extension . [ 16 ] Mas di 99 pa e total di tur e sorto ku un biaha ordenámi riba Tera ku ta trata nan di e extension . [ 17 ] [ 18 ] e Stimulans di Tera aktual di e sorto riba e pago di 10 di 14 miyon di flores , [ 19 ] [ 20 ] di nan di 1,9 miyon e apresio ku a wòrdu nombrá [ 21 ] i 1,6 miyon dokumento un het di dat sentral di e fecha . [ 22 ] Otro frekuentemente , di Mei 2016 , e informacion cientifico di e 1 bill di sorto ta trata den e Tera awor ku solamente ta un milésima parti di un total di escrito . [ 23 ]

(src)="292862"> Evolutionary processes are generally thought of as processes by which these changes occur .
(src)="292863"> Four such processes are widely recognized : natural selection ( in the broad sense , to include sexual selection ) , genetic drift , mutation , and migration ( Fisher 1930 ; Haldane 1932 ) .

(src)="294819"> Evolution
(trg)="2377"> Evolushon
(src)="294820"> Bacteria ( i/bækˈtɪəriə/ ; common noun bacteria , singular bacterium ) constitute a large domain of prokaryotic microorganisms .
(src)="294821"> Typically a few micrometres in length , bacteria have a number of shapes , ranging from spheres to rods and spirals .
(src)="294822"> Bacteria were among the first life forms to appear on Earth , and are present in most of its habitats .
(src)="294823"> Bacteria inhabit soil , water , acidic hot springs , radioactive waste,[4 ] and the deep portions of Earth 's crust .
(src)="294824"> Bacteria also live in symbiotic and parasitic relationships with plants and animals .
(src)="294825"> Most bacteria have not been characterised , and only about half of the bacterial phyla have species that can be grown in the laboratory.[5 ] The study of bacteria is known as bacteriology , a branch of microbiology .
(trg)="2378"> Bakteria  ( i / bæcˈtɪərmi taə / ; )  ta forma un gran parti di e  dominio di  mikroorganismo  prokaryotiko .
(trg)="2379"> Tipikamente algun mikrometer largu , bakteria ta eksisti den varios forma manera esfera , bara i asta spiral .
(trg)="2380"> Bakteria tabata un di e promé formanan di bida ku a aparese riba mundu , i ta presente den mayoria habitat .
(trg)="2381"> Bakteria ta biba den suela , awa , fuente termal asido ,  sushi radioaktivo , [ 4 ] i e partinan di mas hundu di e  mantel di Tera .
(trg)="2382"> Tambe tin bakteria ku ta biba den relashonnan  simbiotiko  o parasitiko  ku mata i bestia .
(trg)="2383"> Gran mayoria di bakteria  no a wordu karakterisa , i solamente mitar di e divishonnan di bakteria  ta kontene sorto ku por wordu kultiva  den laboratorio . [ 5 ] E estudio di bakteria ta konosí komo bakteriologia , i ta un rama di mikrobiologia .
(src)="294826"> There are typically 40 million bacterial cells in a gram of soil and a million bacterial cells in a millilitre of fresh water .
(src)="294827"> There are approximately 5×1030 bacteria on Earth,[6 ] forming a biomass which exceeds that of all plants and animals.[7 ] Bacteria are vital in many stages of the nutrient cycle by recycling nutrients such as the fixation of nitrogen from the atmosphere .
(src)="294828"> The nutrient cycle includes the decomposition of dead bodies and bacteria are responsible for the putrefaction stage in this process.[8 ] In the biological communities surrounding hydrothermal vents and cold seeps , extremophile bacteria provide the nutrients needed to sustain life by converting dissolved compounds , such as hydrogen sulphide and methane , to energy .
(src)="294829"> In March 2013 , data reported by researchers in October 2012 , was published .
(src)="294830"> It was suggested that bacteria thrive in the Mariana Trench , which with a depth of up to 11 kilometres is the deepest known part of the oceans.[9][10 ] Other researchers reported related studies that microbes thrive inside rocks up to 580 metres below the sea floor under 2.6 kilometres of ocean off the coast of the northwestern United States.[9][11 ] According to one of the researchers , " You can find microbes everywhere—they 're extremely adaptable to conditions , and survive wherever they are."[9 ]
(trg)="2384"> Normalmente , tin 40 miyon sel bakterial den un gram di suela i 1 miyon sel bakterial den un mililiter di awa dushi .
(trg)="2385"> Tin aproksimadamente 5 × 1030  bakteria riba mundu , [ 6 ] lokual ta nifika ku nan ta forma un biomasa  ku ta surpasa e biomasa di tur mata i bestia . [ 7 ]  Bakteria  ta vital den hopi etapa di e siklo di nutrishon  dor ku nan ta resikla nutriente den prosesonan manera asimilashon di nitrogeno for di e atmósfera .
(trg)="2386"> E siklo di nutrishon ta inklui e deskomposishon di kadaver ,  i bakteria ta responsabel pa e proseso di putrimentu . [ 8 ] Na komunidat biológikonan rònt di e fuentenan hidrotermal  i fuentenan friu , bakteria extremofilo  ta ofrese e nutrientenan nesesario pa sostene bida dor di komberti supstansianan ku a wordu disolve manera  sulfuro di hidrógeno  ( H2S ) i metan  ( CH4 ) , den energia .
(trg)="2387"> Riba  Mart 2013 , investigadornan a publika datonan ku a wordu reporta riba oktober di 2012 .
(trg)="2388"> E datonan ta  sugerí ku bakteria ta floria den e Mariana Trench , e parti mas hundu di oseano ku  un profundidat di 11 kilometer . [ 9 ] [ 10 ] Otro investigadornan a reporta den estudionan relashona ku mikrobio ta prosperá den baranka te ku 580 meter bou di nivel di laman abou di 2.6 kilometer di oseano for di e kosta di e kantu nortwest di e Estadonan uni di Merka . [ 9 ] [ 11 ] Segun un di e investigadornan , " You can find microbes everywhere — they ' re extremely adaptable to conditions , and survive wherever they are . " ( tradukshon : " Bo por haña e mikrobio tur kaminda- nan ta extremadamente bon den adapta na diferente kondishon , i por sobrebibi unda ku ta . " ) [ 9 ]

(src)="295684"> Signs and symptoms
(trg)="3239"> Síntomanan
(src)="295685"> Diabetes mellitus ( DM ) , commonly referred to as diabetes , is a group of metabolic diseases in which there are high blood sugar levels over a prolonged period.[2 ] Symptoms of high blood sugar include frequent urination , increased thirst , and increased hunger .
(src)="295686"> If left untreated , diabetes can cause many complications.[3 ] Acute complications can include diabetic ketoacidosis , nonketotic hyperosmolar coma , or death.[4 ] Serious long-term complications include heart disease , stroke , chronic kidney failure , foot ulcers , and damage to the eyes.[3 ]
(trg)="3240"> Diabétis Mellitus  ( DM ) , mas miho konosi komo suku den boka di pueblo , ta forma parti di un grupo di malesa metabóliko den kual un nivel haltu di suku ta wòrdu midi den sanger pa un periodo largu . [ 2 ] Síntomanan di suku haltu den sanger ta urina frekuente i mas set i hamber ku normal .
(trg)="3241"> Sin tratamentu diabétis por kousa diferente komplikashon riba termino kortiku i largu .
(trg)="3242"> Komplikashonnan den termino kortiku ta inklui , koma i morto .
(trg)="3243"> Riba termino largu komplikashonnan manera atake selebral , bista ku ta bai atras , malesa di nir króniko i malesa di kurason . 
(src)="295687"> Diabetes is due to either the pancreas not producing enough insulin or the cells of the body not responding properly to the insulin produced.[5 ] There are three main types of diabetes mellitus :
(trg)="3244"> Diabétis ta un konsekuensia di un pankreas ku no ta traha sufisiente insulina òf ora selnan den bo kurpa no réakshona bon riba insulina .  Tin tres tipo prinsipal di diabétis mellitus :
(src)="295688"> Prevention and treatment involve maintaining a healthy diet , regular physical exercise , a normal body weight , and avoiding use of tobacco .
(src)="295689"> Control of blood pressure and maintaining proper foot care are important for people with the disease .
(src)="295690"> Type 1 DM must be managed with insulin injections.[3 ] Type 2 DM may be treated with medications with or without insulin.[7 ] Insulin and some oral medications can cause low blood sugar.[8 ] Weight loss surgery in those with obesity is sometimes an effective measure in those with type 2 DM.[9 ] Gestational diabetes usually resolves after the birth of the baby.[10 ]
(trg)="3245"> Prevenshon i tratamentu di diabétis ta konsistí di un dieta salú , ehersisio regularmente , un peso normal i stop di huma .
(trg)="3246"> DM tipo 1 ta wòrdu tratá dor di inyekshon di insulina .
(trg)="3247"> DM tipo 2 por wòrdu tratá ku inyekshon di insulina pa baha nivel di suku den sanger .
(trg)="3248"> Den algun hende ku DM tipo 2 , baha di peso ta un manera efektivo pa manehá e malesa aki .
(trg)="3249"> Hende muhé embarasá ku ta desaroyá  diabétis durante nan embaraso ta rekupera mesora despues di nasementu di e yu .
(src)="295691"> The classic symptoms of untreated diabetes are weight loss , polyuria ( increased urination ) , polydipsia ( increased thirst ) , and polyphagia ( increased hunger).[18 ] Symptoms may develop rapidly ( weeks or months ) in type  1 DM , while they usually develop much more slowly and may be subtle or absent in type  2 DM .
(trg)="3250"> Síntomanan di diabétis sin tratamentu ta : baha di peso , urina hopi ( mas ku normal ) , hopi set i hamber .
(trg)="3251"> Den DM tipo 1 e síntomanan aki ta desaroya rapidamente ( dentro di siman òf luna ) .
(trg)="3252"> Al kontrario , den DM tipo 2 nan ta desaroya poko poko i den sièrto kaso nan ta ousente .
(src)="295695"> Type 1 DM results from the pancreas 's failure to produce enough insulin .
(src)="295696"> This form was previously referred to as " insulin-dependent diabetes mellitus " ( IDDM ) or " juvenile diabetes " .
(src)="295697"> The cause is unknown.[3 ] Type 2 DM begins with insulin resistance , a condition in which cells fail to respond to insulin properly.[3 ] As the disease progresses a lack of insulin may also develop.[6 ] This form was previously referred to as " non insulin-dependent diabetes mellitus " ( NIDDM ) or " adult-onset diabetes " .
(src)="295698"> The most common cause is excessive body weight and not enough exercise.[3 ] Gestational diabetes is the third main form and occurs when pregnant women without a previous history of diabetes develop high blood sugar levels.[3 ]
(trg)="3676"> Diabétis tipo 1 ( DM 1 ) ta un konsekuensia di un pankreas ku no ta traha sufisiente insulina .
(trg)="3677"> E motibo pa kual esaki ta sosode no ta konosí .
(trg)="3678"> Diabétis tipo 2 ( DM 2 ) ta un konsekuansia di selnan den bo kurpa ku no ta reakshona bon riba insulina .
(trg)="3679"> E di tres forma di diabétis ta okurí den hende muhe embarasá , ku prome ku nan embaraso no ta tin diabétis , ku ta desaroya un nivel haltu di suku den sanger .
